The barriers\n * are emitted by the sources when instructed to do so by the JobManager. When operators receive a\n * CheckpointBarrier on one of its inputs, it knows that this is the point between the\n * pre-checkpoint and post-checkpoint data.\n *\n * <p>Once an operator has received a checkpoint barrier from all its input channels, it knows that\n * a certain checkpoint is complete. It can trigger the operator specific checkpoint behavior and\n * broadcast the barrier to downstream operators.\n *\n * <p>Depending on the semantic guarantees, may hold off post-checkpoint data until the checkpoint\n * is complete (exactly once).\n *\n * <p>The checkpoint barrier IDs are strictly monotonous increasing.\n */\npublic class CheckpointBarrier extends RuntimeEvent {\n\n    private final long id;\n    private final long timestamp;\n    private final CheckpointOptions checkpointOptions;\n\n    public CheckpointBarrier(long id, long timestamp, CheckpointOptions checkpointOptions) {\n        this.id = id;\n        this.timestamp = timestamp;\n        this.checkpointOptions = checkNotNull(checkpointOptions);\n    }\n\n    public long getId() {\n        return id;\n    }\n\n    public long getTimestamp() {\n        return timestamp;\n    }\n\n    public CheckpointOptions getCheckpointOptions() {\n        return checkpointOptions;\n    }\n\n    public CheckpointBarrier withOptions(CheckpointOptions checkpointOptions) {\n        return this.checkpointOptions == checkpointOptions\n                ? this\n                : new CheckpointBarrier(id, timestamp, checkpointOptions);\n    }\n\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Serialization\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    //\n    //  These methods are inherited form the generic serialization of AbstractEvent\n    //  but would require the CheckpointBarrier to be mutable. It also collects and maintains the overview of the state handles reported by\n * the tasks that acknowledge the checkpoint.\n */\npublic class CheckpointCoordinator {\n\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(CheckpointCoordinator.class);\n\n    /** The number of recent checkpoints whose IDs are remembered. */\n    private static final int NUM_GHOST_CHECKPOINT_IDS = 16;\n\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /** Coordinator-wide lock to safeguard the checkpoint updates. */\n    private final Object lock = new Object();\n\n    /** The job whose checkpoint this coordinator coordinates. */\n    private final JobID job;\n\n    /** Default checkpoint properties. */\n    private final CheckpointProperties checkpointProperties;\n\n    /** The executor used for asynchronous calls, like potentially blocking I/O. */\n    private final Executor executor;\n\n    private final CheckpointsCleaner checkpointsCleaner;\n\n    /** The operator coordinators that need to be checkpointed. */\n    private final Collection<OperatorCoordinatorCheckpointContext> coordinatorsToCheckpoint;\n\n    /** Map from checkpoint ID to the pending checkpoint. */\n    @GuardedBy(\"lock\")\n    private final Map<Long, PendingCheckpoint> pendingCheckpoints;\n\n    /**\n     * Completed checkpoints. Implementations can be blocking. Make sure calls to methods accessing\n     * this don't block the job manager actor and run asynchronously.\n     */\n    private final CompletedCheckpointStore completedCheckpointStore;\n\n    /**\n     * The root checkpoint state backend, which is responsible for initializing the checkpoint,\n     * storing the metadata, and cleaning up the checkpoint.\n     */\n    private final CheckpointStorageCoordinatorView checkpointStorageView;\n\n    /** A list of recent expired checkpoint IDs, to identify late messages (vs invalid ones). */\n    private final ArrayDeque<Long> recentExpiredCheckpoints;\n\n    /**\n     * Checkpoint ID counter to ensure ascending IDs. In case of job manager failures, these need to\n     * be ascending across job managers.","numLines":150,"startLine":1,"totalLines":2453}}}

   public void checkpointState(\n            CheckpointMetaData metadata,\n            CheckpointOptions options,\n            CheckpointMetricsBuilder metrics,\n            OperatorChain<?, ?> operatorChain,\n            boolean isTaskFinished,\n            Supplier<Boolean> isRunning)\n            throws Exception {\n\n        checkNotNull(options);\n        checkNotNull(metrics);\n\n        // All of the following steps happen as an atomic step from the perspective of barriers and\n        // records/watermarks/timers/callbacks.\n        // We generally try to emit the checkpoint barrier as soon as possible to not affect\n        // downstream\n        // checkpoint alignments\n\n        if (lastCheckpointId >= metadata.getCheckpointId()) {\n            LOG.info(\n                    \"Out of order checkpoint barrier (aborted previously?): {} >= {}\",\n                    lastCheckpointId,\n                    metadata.getCheckpointId());\n            channelStateWriter.abort(metadata.getCheckpointId(), new CancellationException(), true);\n            checkAndClearAbortedStatus(metadata.getCheckpointId());\n            return;\n        }\n\n        logCheckpointProcessingDelay(metadata);\n\n        // Step (0): Record the last triggered checkpointId and abort the sync phase of checkpoint\n        // if necessary.\n        lastCheckpointId = metadata.getCheckpointId();\n        if (checkAndClearAbortedStatus(metadata.getCheckpointId())) {\n            // broadcast cancel checkpoint marker to avoid downstream back-pressure due to\n            // checkpoint barrier align.\n            operatorChain.broadcastEvent(new CancelCheckpointMarker(metadata.getCheckpointId()));\n            channelStateWriter.abort(\n                    metadata.getCheckpointId(),\n                    new CancellationException(\"checkpoint aborted via notification\"),\n                    true);\n            LOG.info(\n                    \"Checkpoint {} has been notified as aborted, would not trigger any checkpoint.\",\n                    metadata.getCheckpointId());\n            return;\n        }\n\n        if (fileMergingSnapshotManager != null) {\n            // notify file merging snapshot manager for managed dir lifecycle management\n            fileMergingSnapshotManager.notifyCheckpointStart(\n                    FileMergingSnapshotManager.SubtaskKey.of(env), metadata.getCheckpointId());\n        }\n\n        // if checkpoint has been previously unaligned, but was forced to be aligned (pointwise\n        // connection), revert it here so that it can jump over output data\n        if (options.getAlignment() == CheckpointOptions.AlignmentType.FORCED_ALIGNED) {\n            options = options.withUnalignedSupported();\n            initInputsCheckpoint(metadata.getCheckpointId(), options);\n        }\n\n        // Step (1): Prepare the checkpoint, allow operators to do some pre-barrier work.\n        //           The pre-barrier work should be nothing or minimal in the common case.\n        operatorChain.prepareSnapshotPreBarrier(metadata.getCheckpointId());\n\n        // Step (2): Send the checkpoint barrier downstream\n        LOG.debug(\n                \"Task {} broadcastEvent at {}, triggerTime {}, passed time {}\",\n                taskName,\n                System.currentTimeMillis(),\n                metadata.getTimestamp(),\n                System.currentTimeMillis() - metadata.getTimestamp());\n        CheckpointBarrier checkpointBarrier =\n                new CheckpointBarrier(metadata.getCheckpointId(), metadata.getTimestamp(), options);\n        operatorChain.broadcastEvent(checkpointBarrier, options.isUnalignedCheckpoint());\n\n        // Step (3): Register alignment timer to timeout aligned barrier to unaligned barrier\n        registerAlignmentTimer(metadata.getCheckpointId(), operatorChain, checkpointBarrier);\n\n        // Step (4): Prepare to spill the in-flight buffers for input and output\n        if (options.needsChannelState()) {\n            // output data already written while broadcasting event\n            channelStateWriter.finishOutput(metadata.getCheckpointId());\n        }\n\n        // Step (5): Take the state snapshot. CollectionUtil.newHashMapWithExpectedSize(operatorChain.getNumberOfOperators());\n        try {\n            if (takeSnapshotSync(\n                    snapshotFutures, metadata, metrics, options, operatorChain, isRunning)) {\n                finishAndReportAsync(\n                        snapshotFutures,\n                        metadata,\n                        metrics,\n                        operatorChain.isTaskDeployedAsFinished(),\n                        isTaskFinished,\n                        isRunning);\n            } else {\n                cleanup(snapshotFutures, metadata, Let me now write the analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md`.\n\nHere's what I've learned:\n\n1. **CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()** - Entrypoint for checkpoint. Called either periodically via a timer or externally. It:\n   - Creates a `CheckpointTriggerRequest`\n   - Calls `startTriggeringCheckpoint()`\n   - Calculates `CheckpointPlan`\n   - Gets checkpoint ID from `CheckpointIDCounter`\n   - Creates `PendingCheckpoint`\n   - Initializes `CheckpointStorageLocation`\n   - Triggers `OperatorCoordinator` checkpoints\n   - Snapshots master states\n   - Then calls `triggerTasks()` → `triggerCheckpointRequest()` → `triggerTasks()`\n\n2. **Execution.triggerCheckpoint()** - For each source task in the checkpoint plan, delegates to `TaskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint()` via RPC\n\n3. **TaskExecutor.triggerCheckpoint()** - Receives the RPC, retrieves the `Task` by execution attempt ID, and invokes the checkpoint trigger on that task\n\n4. **Task.triggerCheckpointBarrier()** - Queues a checkpoint action on the mailbox through `CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()`\n\n5. **StreamTask/SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState()** - Executes the core task-side checkpoint sequence: prepares the snapshot pre-barrier, broadcasts the checkpoint barrier downstream to operators, registers an alignment timer, spills any in-flight buffers for unaligned checkpoints, and takes a synchronous state snapshot before moving to async finalization\n\n6. **AsyncCheckpointRunnable** - Materializes the state handles and reports completion back through the task state manager, which sends an `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC to the JobManager\n\n7. **CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()** - Collects task acknowledgments and triggers completion logic once all tasks have responded\n\n8. **completePendingCheckpoint()** - Writes checkpoint metadata to storage, creates a `CompletedCheckpoint` object, stores it, and notifies all tasks that the checkpoint is finalized\n\nFor downstream tasks receiving a barrier, the aligned barrier handler uses a state machine that blocks input channels and waits for barriers from all sources before triggering the checkpoint.\n\nThe at-least-once tracker doesn't block but monitors when all barriers for a checkpoint ID arrive, while the unaligned handler triggers immediately on the first barrier and uses a coordinator to spill any in-flight data.\n\nA `PendingCheckpoint` is created when triggering starts, tracks which tasks haven't acknowledged yet, and removes them from that map as acknowledgments arrive.\n\nOnce all tasks acknowledge, the checkpoint finalizes by writing metadata and creating a `CompletedCheckpoint`. The whole system follows a two-phase commit pattern where barriers propagate and snapshots happen first, then the coordinator completes the checkpoint and notifies tasks. It uses state machines to manage barrier collection, observers to notify tasks, async runnables to decouple snapshot work from task execution, and a template method pattern for the barrier handler offsets)\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns\n\n**Distributed Two-Phase Commit (2PC)**\nThe checkpoint protocol is a form of 2PC:\n- *Phase 1 (voting/prepare)*: `CheckpointCoordinator` triggers source tasks, which inject `CheckpointBarrier` events into the data stream. Each downstream task, upon receiving barriers from all input channels, takes a local snapshot and sends an `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC back to `CheckpointCoordinator`.\n- *Phase 2 (commit)*: Once all tasks have acknowledged (`PendingCheckpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()`), `CheckpointCoordinator` finalizes the metadata and calls `sendAcknowledgeMessages` to notify all tasks to commit (e.g., externally via Kafka commit). The completion is atomic in the coordinator, but distributed task commits happen subsequently.\n\n**State Machine Pattern (Barrier Handler States)**\n`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` implements barrier alignment via a `BarrierHandlerState` interface:\n- **Aligned mode**: `WaitingForFirstBarrier` → (first barrier arrives) → `CollectingBarriers` (blocks that input channel) → (all barriers received) → triggers checkpoint, returns to `WaitingForFirstBarrier`\n- **Unaligned mode**: `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned` → triggers checkpoint on first barrier, immediately, without blocking; spills in-flight data to checkpoint storage\n- **Alternating mode**: Begins as aligned; if alignment timeout expires, transitions to unaligned mid-checkpoint\n\n**Observer / Callback Pattern**\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` holds a reference to `CheckpointableTask` (implemented by `StreamTask`) and invokes `triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` once alignment is complete. This decouples barrier-tracking logic from snapshot execution.\n\n**Async Execution Pattern**\n`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()` performs a minimal synchronous phase (barrier broadcast + initiate snapshots), then submits an `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` to a thread pool. The async phase awaits state handle futures, serializes them, and sends the ACK. This allows task processing to continue while state is persisted.\n\n**Mailbox / Actor Model**\n`StreamTask` uses a single-threaded mailbox executor. `Task.triggerCheckpointBarrier()` submits the checkpoint action to the mailbox queue via `triggerCheckpointAsync()`, ensuring the checkpoint runs in the same thread as record processing (avoiding data races).\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|---|---|\n| `CheckpointCoordinator` | Global orchestration: trigger, track pending, receive ACKs, finalize, store, notify commit |\n| `PendingCheckpoint` | Mutable state for an in-progress checkpoint: tracks outstanding ACKs, collects operator states |\n| `CompletedCheckpoint` | Immutable record with all operator state handles and external metadata pointer |\n| `CheckpointIDCounter` | Generates globally ascending checkpoint IDs (ZooKeeper-backed in HA) |\n| `CheckpointPlan` | Describes which tasks are triggered, awaited, and committed to |\n| `Execution` | Single attempt lifecycle: dispatches RPC trigger to its assigned TaskManager |\n| `TaskExecutorGateway` | RPC interface from JobManager to TaskManager |\n| `Task` | TaskManager-side task lifecycle; routes trigger from RPC thread to mailbox |\n| `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl` | Task-side protocol: prepares, broadcasts barrier, coordinates snapshot, reports async |\n| `OperatorChain` | Manages operator chain; relays barrier broadcast and snapshot to each operator |\n| `CheckpointedInputGate` | Input side: intercepts `CheckpointBarrier` events from network, routes to `CheckpointBarrierHandler` |\n| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` | Exactly-once barrier alignment (aligned and unaligned modes) |\n| `CheckpointBarrierTracker` | At-least-once barrier counting (no blocking) |\n| `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` | Materializes state, reports completion to `TaskStateManagerImpl` |\n| `CheckpointResponder` | Interface for task→coordinator ACK/decline messages |\n| `CompletedCheckpointStore` | Persists completed checkpoints; manages retention and subsumption |\n\n### Data Flow Description\n\n```\nJobManager (CheckpointCoordinator)\n  │\n  │ 1. calculateCheckpointPlan() → source tasks identified\n  │ 2. createPendingCheckpoint() → registered in pendingCheckpoints map\n  │ 3. OperatorCoordinator checkpoints\n  │ 4. triggerTasks() → for each source Execution:\n  │\n  ▼\nExecution.triggerCheckpoint()\n  │ via TaskManagerGateway RPC\n  ▼\nTaskExecutor.triggerCheckpoint()\n  │ → task.triggerCheckpointBarrier()\n  ▼\nTask (mailbox)\n  │ → StreamTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()\n  ▼\nSubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()\n  │ 1. prepareSnapshotPreBarrier()\n  │ 2. operatorChain.broadcastEvent(CheckpointBarrier)  ──────────────────────┐\n  │ 3. register alignment timer                                                │ barrier flows through\n  │ 4. finishOutput() [unaligned: spill in-flight data]                        │ network channels\n  │ 5. takeSnapshotSync() → operatorChain.snapshotState()                      │\n  │                                                                             ▼\n  │                                              Downstream Task (CheckpointedInputGate)\n  │                                                │ intercepts CheckpointBarrier\n  │                                                ▼\n  │                                            CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()\n  │                                                │\n  │                               ┌────────────────┴─────────────────┐\n  │                               │ Aligned (SingleCheckpoint)        │ At-least-once (Tracker)\n  │                               │ WaitingForFirstBarrier            │ counts barriers\n  │                               │  → blocks channel                 │ no blocking\n  │                               │ CollectingBarriers                │ when count == N:\n  │                               │  → waits all N channels           │ notifyCheckpoint()\n  │                               │ → notifyCheckpoint()              │\n  │                               └─────────────────┬─────────────────┘\n  │                                                 │ triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()\n  │                                                 ▼\n  │                                      SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()\n  │                                      (same 5-step process, broadcasts barrier further)\n  │\n  ▼\nAsyncCheckpointRunnable (async thread pool)\n  │ awaits OperatorSnapshotFutures\n  │ reportCompletedSnapshotStates()\n  ▼\nTaskStateManagerImpl.reportTaskStateSnapshots()\n  │\n  ▼\nCheckpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint()   [RPC back to JobManager]\n  │\n  ▼\nJobManager (CheckpointCoordinator)\nCheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()\n  │ → PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()\n  │   removes from notYetAcknowledgedTasks\n  │\n  │ when isFullyAcknowledged():\n  ▼\nCheckpointCoordinator.completePendingCheckpoint()\n  │ → PendingCheckpoint.finalizeCheckpoint()\n  │     writes CheckpointMetadata to storage\n  │     creates CompletedCheckpoint\n  │ → CompletedCheckpointStore.addCheckpointAndSubsumeOldest()\n  │ → sendAcknowledgeMessages() → tasks call notifyCheckpointComplete()\n  │     (commit phase: e.g., Kafka offset commit)\n```\n\n### Interface Contracts Between Components\n\n- **CheckpointCoordinator ↔ Execution**: `Execution.triggerCheckpoint()` returns `CompletableFuture<Acknowledge>` — only confirms the trigger was received by TaskManager, NOT that the checkpoint completed\n- **TaskExecutorGateway.triggerCheckpoint()**: RPC that delivers the trigger from JobManager to TaskManager; returns `Acknowledge` on receipt\n- **CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()**: Async invocation on the mailbox thread; returns `CompletableFuture<Boolean>` indicating trigger success\n- **CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint()** → **CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()**: Synchronous callback on the task thread; must not block\n- **CheckpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint()**: RPC from TaskManager back to JobManager carrying `TaskStateSnapshot` (all operator state handles) and `CheckpointMetrics`\n- **PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()**: Returns `TaskAcknowledgeResult` enum (`SUCCESS`, `DUPLICATE`, `UNKNOWN`, `DISCARDED`) to handle idempotency and late messages\n\n### Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoint Handling\n\n**Aligned Checkpoints (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler, aligned factory)**\n- Initial state: `WaitingForFirstBarrier`\n- On first barrier from any channel: block that channel (stop consuming), transition to `CollectingBarriers`\n- On each subsequent barrier: block that channel, add to `alignedChannels`\n- When `alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`: mark alignment end, call `notifyCheckpoint()`, reset state\n- Effect: upstream data is buffered/backpressured; ensures a clean cut-point with no in-flight records\n\n**Unaligned Checkpoints (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler, unaligned factory)**\n- Initial state: `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`\n- On first barrier from any channel: immediately trigger checkpoint (do not block any channel)\n- In-flight data in input/output buffers is captured via `ChannelStateWriter` (spilled to checkpoint storage)\n- Barriers are re-emitted immediately when received (no waiting for other channels)\n- Effect: no backpressure stall; higher checkpoint overhead due to in-flight buffer capture\n\n**Alternating Mode (default in production)**\n- Starts as aligned; if `alignedCheckpointTimeout` expires during alignment, transitions to unaligned mid-flight\n- Provides the latency guarantees of aligned checkpoints under low load, and the progress guarantees of unaligned under high load\n\n**CheckpointBarrierTracker (at-least-once)**\n- No channel blocking; maintains a queue of `CheckpointBarrierCount` objects\n- When barrier count for a checkpoint ID reaches `targetChannelCount`, calls `notifyCheckpoint()`\n- Allows data records from post-barrier channels to pass through before snapshot completes → at-least-once semantics\n\n### PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle\n\n1. **Created**: `CheckpointCoordinator.createPendingCheckpoint()` — populates `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` from `CheckpointPlan.getTasksToWaitFor()`; stored in `pendingCheckpoints` map under checkpoint ID; cancellation timer scheduled\n2. **Collecting ACKs**: Each `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC removes an entry from `notYetAcknowledgedTasks`, adds to `acknowledgedTasks`, merges `OperatorSubtaskState` into `operatorStates` map\n3. **Fully acknowledged**: `isFullyAcknowledged()` = tasks + coordinators + master states all done\n4. **Finalized**: `finalizeCheckpoint()` writes `CheckpointMetadata` (operator states + master states) to the storage location, returns `CompletedCheckpoint`; `PendingCheckpoint` is disposed\n5. **Persisted**: `CompletedCheckpoint` added to `CompletedCheckpointStore`; old checkpoints subsumed\n6. **Notified**: `sendAcknowledgeMessages()` notifies all tasks → they invoke `notifyCheckpointComplete()` for commit-phase side effects\n7. **Failure paths**: Timeout fires → `abortPendingCheckpoint()`; any `DeclineCheckpoint` → same; all pending checkpoints with lower IDs are subsumed when a higher one completes\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nFlink's checkpoint coordination implements a distributed two-phase commit where the JobManager's `CheckpointCoordinator` initiates Phase 1 by triggering source tasks via RPC (`Execution.triggerCheckpoint` → `TaskExecutorGateway.triggerCheckpoint` → `Task.triggerCheckpointBarrier`), which inject `CheckpointBarrier` events into the data stream; downstream tasks align these memory); subsumed checkpoints are cleaned up\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Entry point**: `CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint(CheckpointProperties, ...)` (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:619`)\n2. **Queues/executes**: `CheckpointCoordinator.startTriggeringCheckpoint(CheckpointTriggerRequest)` (`:630`) — guards concurrency with `isTriggering` flag\n3. globally monotonically increasing checkpoint ID\n5. **Creates state**: `CheckpointCoordinator.createPendingCheckpoint(...)` (`:901`) — instantiates `PendingCheckpoint` and registers in (`:836`) → `Execution.triggerCheckpoint(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)` (`:1070`) for each task in `checkpointPlan.getTasksToTrigger()`\n10. **RPC dispatch**: (`:752`) — synchronously initiates state snapshots for all operators in the chain\n14. **Async completion**: `finishAndReportAsync(...)` (`:690`) — submits `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` to async thread pool; awaits completion of all operator state futures\n15. **Barrier received downstream**: `CheckpointedInputGate.pollNext()` intercepts `CheckpointBarrier` event (`:180`) → `alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`, fires `notifyCheckpoint(trigger)` (`:287`)\n17. **Downstream snapshot triggered**: `CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint(checkpointBarrier)` (`:125`) → `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier(checkpointMetaData, options, metrics)` (`:147`) — loops back to step 13 for non-source tasks\n18. **ACK sent**: **Notify commit**: `CheckpointCoordinator.sendAcknowledgeMessages(tasksToCommitTo, ...)` (`:1439`) — sends `notifyCheckpointComplete` to all tasks so they can commit external side effects (e.g. Kafka offsets)\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns\n\n**Distributed Two-Phase Commit (2PC)**\nThe checkpoint protocol is a form of 2PC:\n- *Phase 1 (voting/prepare)*: `CheckpointCoordinator` triggers source tasks, which inject `CheckpointBarrier` events into the data stream. Each downstream task, upon receiving barriers from all input channels, takes a local snapshot and sends an `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC back to `CheckpointCoordinator`.\n- *Phase 2 (commit)*: Once all tasks have acknowledged (`PendingCheckpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()`), `CheckpointCoordinator` finalizes the metadata and calls `sendAcknowledgeMessages` to notify all tasks to commit (e.g., externally via Kafka commit). The completion is atomic in the coordinator, but distributed task commits happen subsequently.\n\n**State Machine Pattern (Barrier Handler States)**\n`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` implements barrier alignment via a `BarrierHandlerState` interface:\n- **Aligned mode**: `WaitingForFirstBarrier` → (first barrier arrives) → `CollectingBarriers` (blocks that input channel) → (all barriers received) → triggers checkpoint, returns to `WaitingForFirstBarrier`\n- **Unaligned mode**: `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned` → triggers checkpoint on first barrier, immediately, without blocking; spills in-flight data to checkpoint storage\n- **Alternating mode**: Begins as aligned; if alignment timeout expires, transitions to unaligned mid-checkpoint\n\n**Observer / Callback Pattern**\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` holds a reference to `CheckpointableTask` (implemented by `StreamTask`) and invokes `triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` once alignment is complete. This decouples barrier-tracking logic from snapshot execution.\n\n**Async Execution Pattern**\n`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()` performs a minimal synchronous phase (barrier broadcast + initiate snapshots), then submits an `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` to a thread pool. The async phase awaits state handle futures, serializes them, and sends the ACK. This allows task processing to continue while state is persisted.\n\n**Mailbox / Actor Model**\n`StreamTask` uses a single-threaded mailbox executor. `Task.triggerCheckpointBarrier()` submits the checkpoint action to the mailbox queue via `triggerCheckpointAsync()`, ensuring the checkpoint runs in the same thread as record processing (avoiding data races).\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|---|---|\n| `CheckpointCoordinator` | Global orchestration: trigger, track pending, receive ACKs, finalize, store, notify commit |\n| `PendingCheckpoint` | Mutable state for an in-progress checkpoint: tracks outstanding ACKs, collects operator states |\n| `CompletedCheckpoint` | Immutable record with all operator state handles and external metadata pointer |\n| `CheckpointIDCounter` | Generates globally ascending checkpoint IDs (ZooKeeper-backed in HA) |\n| `CheckpointPlan` | Describes which tasks are triggered, awaited, and committed to |\n| `Execution` | Single attempt lifecycle: dispatches RPC trigger to its assigned TaskManager |\n| `TaskExecutorGateway` | RPC interface from JobManager to TaskManager |\n| `Task` | TaskManager-side task lifecycle; routes trigger from RPC thread to mailbox |\n| `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl` | Task-side protocol: prepares, broadcasts barrier, coordinates snapshot, reports async |\n| `OperatorChain` | Manages operator chain; relays barrier broadcast and snapshot to each operator |\n| `CheckpointedInputGate` | Input side: intercepts `CheckpointBarrier` events from network, routes to `CheckpointBarrierHandler` |\n| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` | Exactly-once barrier alignment (aligned and unaligned modes) |\n| `CheckpointBarrierTracker` | At-least-once barrier counting (no blocking) |\n| `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` | Materializes state, reports completion to `TaskStateManagerImpl` |\n| `CheckpointResponder` | Interface for task→coordinator ACK/decline messages |\n| `CompletedCheckpointStore` | Persists completed checkpoints; manages retention and subsumption |\n\n### Data Flow Description\n\n```\nJobManager (CheckpointCoordinator)\n  │\n  │ 1. calculateCheckpointPlan() → source tasks identified\n  │ 2. createPendingCheckpoint() → registered in pendingCheckpoints map\n  │ 3. OperatorCoordinator checkpoints\n  │ 4. triggerTasks() → for each source Execution:\n  │\n  ▼\nExecution.triggerCheckpoint()\n  │ via TaskManagerGateway RPC\n  ▼\nTaskExecutor.triggerCheckpoint()\n  │ → task.triggerCheckpointBarrier()\n  ▼\nTask (mailbox)\n  │ → StreamTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()\n  ▼\nSubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()\n  │ 1. prepareSnapshotPreBarrier()\n  │ 2. operatorChain.broadcastEvent(CheckpointBarrier)  ──────────────────────┐\n  │ 3. register alignment timer                                                │ barrier flows through\n  │ 4. finishOutput() [unaligned: spill in-flight data]                        │ network channels\n  │ 5. takeSnapshotSync() → operatorChain.snapshotState()                      │\n  │                                                                             ▼\n  │                                              Downstream Task (CheckpointedInputGate)\n  │                                                │ intercepts CheckpointBarrier\n  │                                                ▼\n  │                                            CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()\n  │                                                │\n  │                               ┌────────────────┴─────────────────┐\n  │                               │ Aligned (SingleCheckpoint)        │ At-least-once (Tracker)\n  │                               │ WaitingForFirstBarrier            │ counts barriers\n  │                               │  → blocks channel                 │ no blocking\n  │                               │ CollectingBarriers                │ when count == N:\n  │                               │  → waits all N channels           │ notifyCheckpoint()\n  │                               │ → notifyCheckpoint()              │\n  │                               └─────────────────┬─────────────────┘\n  │                                                 │ triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()\n  │                                                 ▼\n  │                                      SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()\n  │                                      (same 5-step process, broadcasts barrier further)\n  │\n  ▼\nAsyncCheckpointRunnable (async thread pool)\n  │ awaits OperatorSnapshotFutures\n  │ reportCompletedSnapshotStates()\n  ▼\nTaskStateManagerImpl.reportTaskStateSnapshots()\n  │\n  ▼\nCheckpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint()   [RPC back to JobManager]\n  │\n  ▼\nJobManager (CheckpointCoordinator)\nCheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()\n  │ → PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()\n  │   removes from notYetAcknowledgedTasks\n  │\n  │ when isFullyAcknowledged():\n  ▼\nCheckpointCoordinator.completePendingCheckpoint()\n  │ → PendingCheckpoint.finalizeCheckpoint()\n  │     writes CheckpointMetadata to storage\n  │     creates CompletedCheckpoint\n  │ → CompletedCheckpointStore.addCheckpointAndSubsumeOldest()\n  │ → sendAcknowledgeMessages() → tasks call notifyCheckpointComplete()\n  │     (commit phase: e.g., Kafka offset commit)\n```\n\n### Interface Contracts Between Components\n\n- **CheckpointCoordinator ↔ Execution**: `Execution.triggerCheckpoint()` returns `CompletableFuture<Acknowledge>` — only confirms the trigger was received by TaskManager, NOT that the checkpoint completed\n- **TaskExecutorGateway.triggerCheckpoint()**: RPC that delivers the trigger from JobManager to TaskManager; returns `Acknowledge` on receipt\n- **CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()**: Async invocation on the mailbox thread; returns `CompletableFuture<Boolean>` indicating trigger success\n- **CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint()** → **CheckpointableTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()**: Synchronous callback on the task thread; must not block\n- **CheckpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint()**: RPC from TaskManager back to JobManager carrying `TaskStateSnapshot` (all operator state handles) and `CheckpointMetrics`\n- **PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()**: Returns `TaskAcknowledgeResult` enum (`SUCCESS`, `DUPLICATE`, `UNKNOWN`, `DISCARDED`) to handle idempotency and late messages\n\n### Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoint Handling\n\n**Aligned Checkpoints (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler, aligned factory)**\n- Initial state: `WaitingForFirstBarrier`\n- On first barrier from any channel: block that channel (stop consuming), transition to `CollectingBarriers`\n- On each subsequent barrier: block that channel, add to `alignedChannels`\n- When `alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`: mark alignment end, call `notifyCheckpoint()`, reset state\n- Effect: upstream data is buffered/backpressured; ensures a clean cut-point with no in-flight records\n\n**Unaligned Checkpoints (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler, unaligned factory)**\n- Initial state: `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`\n- On first barrier from any channel: immediately trigger checkpoint (do not block any channel)\n- In-flight data in input/output buffers is captured via `ChannelStateWriter` (spilled to checkpoint storage)\n- Barriers are re-emitted immediately when received (no waiting for other channels)\n- Effect: no backpressure stall; higher checkpoint overhead due to in-flight buffer capture\n\n**Alternating Mode (default in production)**\n- Starts as aligned; if `alignedCheckpointTimeout` expires during alignment, transitions to unaligned mid-flight\n- Provides the latency guarantees of aligned checkpoints under low load, and the progress guarantees of unaligned under high load\n\n**CheckpointBarrierTracker (at-least-once)**\n- No channel blocking; maintains a queue of `CheckpointBarrierCount` objects\n- When barrier count for a checkpoint ID reaches `targetChannelCount`, calls `notifyCheckpoint()`\n- Allows data records from post-barrier channels to pass through before snapshot completes → at-least-once semantics\n\n### PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle\n\n1. **Created**: `CheckpointCoordinator.createPendingCheckpoint()` — populates `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` from `CheckpointPlan.getTasksToWaitFor()`; stored in `pendingCheckpoints` map under checkpoint ID; cancellation timer scheduled\n2. **Collecting ACKs**: Each `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC removes an entry from `notYetAcknowledgedTasks`, adds to `acknowledgedTasks`, merges `OperatorSubtaskState` into `operatorStates` map\n3. **Fully acknowledged**: `isFullyAcknowledged()` = tasks + coordinators + master states all done\n4. **Finalized**: `finalizeCheckpoint()` writes `CheckpointMetadata` (operator states + master states) to the storage location, returns `CompletedCheckpoint`; `PendingCheckpoint` is disposed\n5. **Persisted**: `CompletedCheckpoint` added to `CompletedCheckpointStore`; old checkpoints subsumed\n6. **Notified**: `sendAcknowledgeMessages()` notifies all tasks → they invoke `notifyCheckpointComplete()` for commit-phase side effects\n7. **Failure paths**: Timeout fires → `abortPendingCheckpoint()`; any `DeclineCheckpoint` → same; all pending checkpoints with lower IDs are subsumed when a higher one completes\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nFlink's checkpoint coordination implements a distributed two-phase commit where the JobManager's `CheckpointCoordinator` initiates Phase 1 by triggering source tasks via RPC (`Execution.triggerCheckpoint` → `TaskExecutorGateway.triggerCheckpoint` → `Task.triggerCheckpointBarrier`), which inject `CheckpointBarrier` events into the data stream; downstream tasks align these barriers using either `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (exactly-once, blocking channels until all barriers arrive) or `CheckpointBarrierTracker` (at-least-once, counting without blocking), then take snapshots and send `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPCs back to the coordinator. The `PendingCheckpoint` accumulates these acknowledgments until fully complete, at which point Phase 2 begins: `completePendingCheckpoint` serializes the metadata to durable storage creating a `CompletedCheckpoint`, and `sendAcknowledgeMessages` notifies all tasks to commit external side effects, completing the global consistent snapshot.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
